(********************************************************

 Internal Street fibrations

 In this file, we define the notion of Street fibration
 internal to a bicategory.

 1. Definition of an internal Street fibration
 2. Lemmas on cartesians
 3. Street fibrations in locally groupoidal bicategories
 4. Morphisms of internal Street fibrations
 5. Cells of internal Street fibrations

 ********************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Categories.

Local Open Scope cat.

(**
1. Definition of an internal Street fibration

We define internal Street fibrations using an unfolded definition.
We also show that it is equivalent to the usual definition of internal Street
fibrations, which is formulated using hom-categories.
 *)
Section InternalStreetFibration.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {e b : B}
          (p : e --> b).

  Definition is_cartesian_2cell_sfib
             {x : B}
             {f g : x --> e}
             (γ : f ==> g)
    : UU
    := ∏ (h : x --> e)
         (α : h ==> g)
         (δp : h · p ==> f · p)
         (q : α ▹ p = δp • (γ ▹ p)),
       ∃! (δ : h ==> f),
       δ ▹ p = δp
       ×
       δ • γ = α.

  Definition is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor
             {x : B}
             {f g : x --> e}
             {γ : f ==> g}
             (Hγ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ)
             {h : x --> e}
             (α : h ==> g)
             (δp : h · p ==> f · p)
             (q : α ▹ p = δp • (γ ▹ p))
    : h ==> f
    := pr11 (Hγ h α δp q).

  Definition is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over
             {x : B}
             {f g : x --> e}
             {γ : f ==> g}
             (Hγ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ)
             {h : x --> e}
             {α : h ==> g}
             {δp : h · p ==> f · p}
             (q : α ▹ p = δp • (γ ▹ p))
    : (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor Hγ _ _ q) ▹ p = δp
    := pr121 (Hγ h α δp q).

  Definition is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_comm
             {x : B}
             {f g : x --> e}
             {γ : f ==> g}
             (Hγ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ)
             {h : x --> e}
             {α : h ==> g}
             {δp : h · p ==> f · p}
             (q : α ▹ p = δp • (γ ▹ p))
    : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor Hγ _ _ q • γ = α
    := pr221 (Hγ h α δp q).

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ
h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: h ==> g
δp: h · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (γ ▹ p)
δ₁, δ₂: h ==> f
pδ₁: δ₁ ▹ p = δp
pδ₂: δ₂ ▹ p = δp
δγ₁: δ₁ • γ = α
δγ₂: δ₂ • γ = α
δ₁ = δ₂

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ
h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: h ==> g
δp: h · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (γ ▹ p)
δ₁, δ₂: h ==> f
pδ₁: δ₁ ▹ p = δp
pδ₂: δ₂ ▹ p = δp
δγ₁: δ₁ • γ = α
δγ₂: δ₂ • γ = α
δ₁ = δ₂

    
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ
h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: h ==> g
δp: h · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (γ ▹ p)
δ₁, δ₂: h ==> f
pδ₁: δ₁ ▹ p = δp
pδ₂: δ₂ ▹ p = δp
δγ₁: δ₁ • γ = α
δγ₂: δ₂ • γ = α
H:= proofirrelevance
  (∑ δ : h ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • γ = α)
  (isapropifcontr (Hγ h α δp q)) (δ₁,, pδ₁,, δγ₁)
  (δ₂,, pδ₂,, δγ₂): δ₁,, pδ₁,, δγ₁ = δ₂,, pδ₂,, δγ₂
δ₁ = δ₂

    exact (maponpaths pr1 H).
  Qed.

f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
γ: f ==> g
isaprop (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ)

  
B: bicat

isaprop (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ)

    
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
γ: f ==> g
t: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
t0: t ==> g
t1: t · p ==> f · p
t2: t0 ▹ p = t1 • (γ ▹ p)
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ _ : t0 ▹ p = t1 • (γ ▹ p),
    ∃! δ : t ==> f, δ ▹ p = t1 × δ • γ = t0) t2)

    apply isapropiscontr.
  Qed.

  Definition internal_sfib_cleaving
    : UU
    := ∏ (x : B)
         (f : x --> b)
         (g : x --> e)
         (α : f ==> g · p),
       ∑ (h : x --> e)
         (γ : h ==> g)
         (β : invertible_2cell (h · p) f),
       is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ
       ×
       γ ▹ p = β • α.

  Definition internal_sfib_cleaving_lift_mor
             (H : internal_sfib_cleaving)
             {x : B}
             {f : x --> b}
             {g : x --> e}
             (α : f ==> g · p)
    : x --> e
    := pr1 (H _ _ _ α).

  Definition internal_sfib_cleaving_lift_cell
             (H : internal_sfib_cleaving)
             {x : B}
             {f : x --> b}
             {g : x --> e}
             (α : f ==> g · p)
    : internal_sfib_cleaving_lift_mor H α ==> g
    := pr12 (H _ _ _ α).

  Definition internal_sfib_cleaving_com
             (H : internal_sfib_cleaving)
             {x : B}
             {f : x --> b}
             {g : x --> e}
             (α : f ==> g · p)
    : invertible_2cell (internal_sfib_cleaving_lift_mor H α · p) f
    := pr122 (H _ _ _ α).

  Definition internal_sfib_cleaving_is_cartesian
             (H : internal_sfib_cleaving)
             {x : B}
             {f : x --> b}
             {g : x --> e}
             (α : f ==> g · p)
    : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib (internal_sfib_cleaving_lift_cell H α)
    := pr1 (pr222 (H _ _ _ α)).

  Definition internal_sfib_cleaving_over
             (H : internal_sfib_cleaving)
             {x : B}
             {f : x --> b}
             {g : x --> e}
             (α : f ==> g · p)
    : internal_sfib_cleaving_lift_cell H α ▹ p
      =
      internal_sfib_cleaving_com H α • α
    := pr2 (pr222 (H _ _ _ α)).

  Definition lwhisker_is_cartesian
    : UU
    := ∏ (x y : B)
         (h : y --> x)
         (f g : x --> e)
         (γ : f ==> g)
         (Hγ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ),
       is_cartesian_2cell_sfib (h ◃ γ).

  Definition internal_sfib
    : UU
    := internal_sfib_cleaving × lwhisker_is_cartesian.

  Coercion internal_sfib_to_cleaving
           (H : internal_sfib)
    : internal_sfib_cleaving
    := pr1 H.

  Definition rep_internal_sfib
    : UU
    := (∏ (x : B),
        street_fib (post_comp x p))
       ×
       (∏ (x y : B)
          (h : y --> x),
        preserves_cartesian
          (post_comp x p)
          (post_comp y p)
          (pre_comp e h)).

internal_sfib

lwhisker_is_cartesian

∑ (h : B ⟦ x, e ⟧) (γ : h ==> g)
(β : invertible_2cell (h · p) f),
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ × γ ▹ p = β • α

Functors.functor_on_morphisms

is_cartesian_2cell_sfib γ × γ ▹ p = β • α

(**
2. Lemmas on cartesians
 *)

B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p (id₂ f)


B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p (id₂ f)

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
∃! δ : g ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • id₂ f = α

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
isaprop (∑ δ : g ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • id₂ f = α)
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
∑ δ : g ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • id₂ f = α

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
isaprop (∑ δ : g ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • id₂ f = α)
 abstract
      (use invproofirrelevance ;
       intros φ₁ φ₂ ;
       use subtypePath ;
       [ intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply cellset_property | ] ;
       exact (!(id2_right _) @ pr22 φ₁ @ !(pr22 φ₂) @ id2_right _)).

e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
∑ δ : g ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • id₂ f = α
 
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
α ▹ p = δp
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
α • id₂ f = α

    
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
α ▹ p = δp
 abstract
        (rewrite q ;
         rewrite id2_rwhisker ;
         apply id2_right).
    
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g ==> f
δp: g · p ==> f · p
q: α ▹ p = δp • (id₂ f ▹ p)
α • id₂ f = α
 abstract
        (apply id2_right).
Defined.

Section VcompIsCartesian.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {e b : B}
          (p : e --> b)
          {x : B}
          {f g h : x --> e}
          {α : f ==> g}
          {β : g ==> h}
          (Hα : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α)
          (Hβ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β).

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g, h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: f ==> g
β: g ==> h
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
k: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: k ==> h
δp: k · p ==> f · p
q: ζ ▹ p = δp • ((α • β) ▹ p)
isaprop (∑ δ : k ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • (α • β) = ζ)

isaprop (∑ δ : k ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • (α • β) = ζ)

isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ δ : k ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • (α • β) = ζ)

B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g, h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: f ==> g
β: g ==> h
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
k: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: k ==> h
δp: k · p ==> f · p
q: ζ ▹ p = δp • ((α • β) ▹ p)
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor p Hβ ζ (δp • (α ▹ p))
  (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k ζ δp q)
▹ p = δp • (α ▹ p)
 apply is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over.
      
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g, h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: f ==> g
β: g ==> h
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
k: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: k ==> h
δp: k · p ==> f · p
q: ζ ▹ p = δp • ((α • β) ▹ p)
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor p Hα
  (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor p Hβ ζ
     (δp • (α ▹ p))
     (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k ζ δp q))
  δp
  (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over p Hβ
     (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k ζ δp q))
▹ p = δp
 apply is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over.

f, g, h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: f ==> g
β: g ==> h
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
k: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: k ==> h
δp: k · p ==> f · p
q: ζ ▹ p = δp • ((α • β) ▹ p)
(λ _ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor p Hα
         (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor p Hβ ζ
            (δp • (α ▹ p))
            (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k
               ζ δp q)) δp
         (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over p Hβ
            (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k
               ζ δp q)) ▹ p = δp,
 is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor p Hα
   (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor p Hβ ζ
      (δp • (α ▹ p))
      (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k ζ δp q))
   δp
   (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over p Hβ
      (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k ζ δp q))
 • (α • β) = ζ)
  (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over p Hα
     (is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_over p Hβ
        (vcomp_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_subproof k ζ δp
           q)))
 abstract
          (simpl ;
           rewrite !vassocr ;
           rewrite !is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_comm ;
           apply idpath).
  Defined.
End VcompIsCartesian.

B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: f ==> g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell α
h: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: h ==> g
δp: h · p ==> f · p
q: ζ ▹ p = δp • (α ▹ p)
∃! δ : h ==> f, δ ▹ p = δp × δ • α = ζ

 abstract
      (use invproofirrelevance ;
       intros φ₁ φ₂ ;
       use subtypePath ;
         [ intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply cellset_property | ] ;
       refine (!(id2_right _) @ _ @ id2_right _) ;
       rewrite <- (vcomp_rinv Hα) ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       rewrite (pr22 φ₁), (pr22 φ₂) ;
       apply idpath).

Section PostComposition.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {e b : B}
          (p : e --> b)
          {x : B}
          {f g h : x --> e}
          (α : f ==> g) {β : g ==> h}
          {γ : f ==> h}
          (Hβ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β)
          (Hγ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p γ)
          (q : α • β = γ).

  Section PostCompositionFactor.
    Context {k : x --> e}
            {δ : k ==> g}
            (δp : k · p ==> f · p)
            (r : δ ▹ p = δp • (α ▹ p)).

k ==> f

Definition map_between_cartesians
           {B : bicat}
           {x e b : B}
           {p : e --> b}
           {g₀ g₁ g₂ : x --> e}
           {α : g₀ ==> g₂}
           (Hα : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α)
           {β : g₁ ==> g₂}
           (Hβ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β)
           (δ : invertible_2cell (g₀ · p) (g₁ · p))
           (r : α ▹ p = δ • (β ▹ p))
  : g₀ ==> g₁
  := is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor _ Hβ α δ r.

Section InvertibleBetweenCartesians.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {x e b : B}
          {p : e --> b}
          {g₀ g₁ g₂ : x --> e}
          {α : g₀ ==> g₂}
          (Hα : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α)
          {β : g₁ ==> g₂}
          (Hβ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β)
          (δ : invertible_2cell (g₀ · p) (g₁ · p))
          (r : α ▹ p = δ • (β ▹ p)).

  Let φ : g₀ ==> g₁ := map_between_cartesians Hα Hβ δ r.

  
B: bicat
x, e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
g₀, g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
α: g₀ ==> g₂
Hα: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p α
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
δ: invertible_2cell (g₀ · p) (g₁ · p)
r: α ▹ p = δ • (β ▹ p)
φ:= map_between_cartesians Hα Hβ δ r: g₀ ==> g₁
β ▹ p = δ ^-1 • (α ▹ p)

β ▹ p = δ ^-1 • (α ▹ p)

  Let ψ : g₁ ==> g₀

β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
δ: invertible_2cell (g₀ · p) (g₁ · p)
r: α ▹ p = δ • (β ▹ p)
φ:= map_between_cartesians Hα Hβ δ r: g₀ ==> g₁
ψ:= map_between_cartesians Hβ Hα
  (inv_of_invertible_2cell δ)
  invertible_between_cartesians_help: g₁ ==> g₀
α ▹ p = id₂ (g₀ · p) • (α ▹ p)

ψ:= map_between_cartesians Hβ Hα
  (inv_of_invertible_2cell δ)
  invertible_between_cartesians_help: g₁ ==> g₀
id₂ g₁ • β = β
 apply id2_left.
  Qed.

B: bicat
x, e, b: B

 exact invertible_between_cartesians_inv₁.
      
B: bicat
x, e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
g₀, g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, e ⟧

  (inv_of_invertible_2cell δ)
  invertible_between_cartesians_help: g₁ ==> g₀
ψ • φ = id₂ g₁
 exact invertible_between_cartesians_inv₂.
  Defined.
End InvertibleBetweenCartesians.

(**
 4. Morphisms of internal Street fibrations
 *)
Definition mor_preserves_cartesian
           {B : bicat}
           {e₁ b₁ : B}
           (p₁ : e₁ --> b₁)
           {e₂ b₂ : B}
           (p₂ : e₂ --> b₂)
           (fe : e₁ --> e₂)
  : UU
  := ∏ (x : B)
       (f g : x --> e₁)
       (γ : f ==> g)
       (Hγ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₁ γ),
     is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₂ (γ ▹ fe).


B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
mor_preserves_cartesian p p (id₁ e)


B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
mor_preserves_cartesian p p (id₁ e)

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
γ: f ==> g
H: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p γ
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p (γ ▹ id₁ e)

  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
γ: f ==> g
H: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p γ
γ ▹ id₁ e = (runitor f • γ) • rinvunitor g

is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p (γ ▹ id₁ e)

H: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p γ
q: γ ▹ id₁ e = (runitor f • γ) • rinvunitor g
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p (runitor f)

      is_iso.

Section Invertible2CellCartesian.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {x e b : B}
          {p p' : e --> b}
          (α : invertible_2cell p p')
          {f g : x --> e}
          {β : f ==> g}
          (Hβ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β)
          {k : x --> e}
          {ζ : k ==> g}
          (δp : k · p' ==> f · p')
          (q : ζ ▹ p' = δp • (β ▹ p')).

  Let δp' : k · p ==> f · p
    := ((k ◃ α) • δp • (f ◃ α^-1)).

  
B: bicat
x, e, b: B
p, p': B ⟦ e, b ⟧
α: invertible_2cell p p'
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
β: f ==> g
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
k: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: k ==> g
δp: k · p' ==> f · p'
q: ζ ▹ p' = δp • (β ▹ p')
δp':= ((k ◃ α) • δp) • (f ◃ α ^-1): k · p ==> f · p
ζ ▹ p = (((k ◃ α) • δp) • (f ◃ α ^-1)) • (β ▹ p)

  
B: bicat
x, e, b: B
p, p': B ⟦ e, b ⟧
α: invertible_2cell p p'
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
β: f ==> g
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
k: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: k ==> g
δp: k · p' ==> f · p'
q: ζ ▹ p' = δp • (β ▹ p')
δp':= ((k ◃ α) • δp) • (f ◃ α ^-1): k · p ==> f · p
ζ ▹ p = (((k ◃ α) • δp) • (f ◃ α ^-1)) • (β ▹ p)

    
B: bicat
x, e, b: B
p, p': B ⟦ e, b ⟧
α: invertible_2cell p p'
f, g: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
β: f ==> g
Hβ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p β
k: B ⟦ x, e ⟧
ζ: k ==> g
δp: k · p' ==> f · p'
q: ζ ▹ p' = δp • (β ▹ p')
δp':= ((k ◃ α) • δp) • (f ◃ α ^-1): k · p ==> f · p
ζ ▹ p = (k ◃ α) • (δp • ((f ◃ α ^-1) • (β ▹ p)))

    
B: bicat
x, e, b: B
p, p': B ⟦ e, b ⟧
α: invertible_2cell p p'

  Definition is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor_inv2cell
    : k ==> f
    := is_cartesian_2cell_sfib_factor
         _ Hβ
         ζ
         ((k ◃ α) • δp • (f ◃ α^-1))
         help_eq.

is_invertible_2cell (k ◃ α)

H: mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe
x: B
f, g: B ⟦ x, e₁ ⟧
γ: f ==> g
Hγ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₁ γ
p: (γ ▹ fe') • (g ◃ α ^-1) = (f ◃ α ^-1) • (γ ▹ fe)
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₂ (γ ▹ fe)
 exact (H x f g γ Hγ).
Defined.


B: bicat
e₁, e₂, b₁, b₂: B
p₁, p₁': B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂, p₂': B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe, fe': B ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell p₁ p₁'
β: invertible_2cell p₂ p₂'
γ: invertible_2cell fe fe'
H: mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe
mor_preserves_cartesian p₁' p₂' fe'


B: bicat
e₁, e₂, b₁, b₂: B
p₁, p₁': B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂, p₂': B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe, fe': B ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell p₁ p₁'
β: invertible_2cell p₂ p₂'
γ: invertible_2cell fe fe'
H: mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe
mor_preserves_cartesian p₁' p₂' fe'

  
B: bicat
e₁, e₂, b₁, b₂: B
p₁, p₁': B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂, p₂': B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧

ζ: h₁ ==> h₂
Hζ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₁' ζ
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₂' (ζ ▹ fe')

Hζ: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₁' ζ
is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₂ (ζ ▹ fe')

p₂, p₂': B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧

  exact Hζ.
Defined.


B: bicat

p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧

  apply (locally_grpd_cartesian HB).

B: bicat
e₁, b₁: B
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
e₂, b₂: B
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: B ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
isaprop (mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe)


B: bicat
e₁, b₁: B
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
e₂, b₂: B
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: B ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
isaprop (mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe)

  
B: bicat
e₁, b₁: B
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
e₂, b₂: B
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: B ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
t: B
t0, t1: B ⟦ t, e₁ ⟧
t2: t0 ==> t1
t3: is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₁ t2
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ _ : is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₁ t2,
    is_cartesian_2cell_sfib p₂ (t2 ▹ fe)) t3)

  exact (isaprop_is_cartesian_2cell_sfib _ _).
Qed.

Definition mor_of_internal_sfib_over
           {B : bicat}
           {e₁ b₁ : B}
           (p₁ : e₁ --> b₁)
           {e₂ b₂ : B}
           (p₂ : e₂ --> b₂)
           (fb : b₁ --> b₂)
  : UU
  := ∑ (fe : e₁ --> e₂),
     mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe
     ×
     invertible_2cell (p₁ · fb) (fe · p₂).

Definition make_mor_of_internal_sfib_over
           {B : bicat}
           {e₁ b₁ : B}
           {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
           {e₂ b₂ : B}
           {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
           {fb : b₁ --> b₂}
           (fe : e₁ --> e₂)
           (fc : mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe)
           (f_com : invertible_2cell (p₁ · fb) (fe · p₂))
  : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
  := (fe ,, fc ,, f_com).

Coercion mor_of_internal_sfib_over_to_mor
         {B : bicat}
         {e₁ b₁ : B}
         {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
         {e₂ b₂ : B}
         {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
         {fb : b₁ --> b₂}
         (fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb)
  : e₁ --> e₂
  := pr1 fe.

Definition mor_of_internal_sfib_over_preserves
           {B : bicat}
           {e₁ b₁ : B}
           {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
           {e₂ b₂ : B}
           {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
           {fb : b₁ --> b₂}
           (fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb)
  : mor_preserves_cartesian p₁ p₂ fe
  := pr12 fe.

Definition mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com
           {B : bicat}
           {e₁ b₁ : B}
           {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
           {e₂ b₂ : B}
           {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
           {fb : b₁ --> b₂}
           (fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb)
  : invertible_2cell (p₁ · fb) (fe · p₂)
  := pr22 fe.


B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
mor_of_internal_sfib_over p p (id₁ b)


B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
mor_of_internal_sfib_over p p (id₁ b)

e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
B ⟦ e, e ⟧
B: bicat

mor_preserves_cartesian p p ?fe
B: bicat

invertible_2cell (p · id₁ b) (?fe · p)

e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
B ⟦ e, e ⟧
 exact (id₁ e).
  
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
mor_preserves_cartesian p p (id₁ e)
 apply id_mor_preserves_cartesian.
  
B: bicat
e, b: B

invertible_2cell (p · id₁ b) (id₁ e · p)
 
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
p · id₁ b ==> id₁ e · p
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
is_invertible_2cell ?η

    
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
p · id₁ b ==> id₁ e · p
 refine (runitor _ • linvunitor _).
    
B: bicat
e, b: B
p: B ⟦ e, b ⟧
is_invertible_2cell (runitor p • linvunitor p)
 is_iso.
Defined.

 exact (comp_preserves_cartesian
             (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_preserves fe₁)
             (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_preserves fe₂)).

e₁, e₂, e₃, b₁, b₂, b₃: B

is_invertible_2cell ?η

    
B: bicat
e₁, e₂, e₃, b₁, b₂, b₃: B
fb₁: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
fb₂: B ⟦ b₂, b₃ ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
p₃: B ⟦ e₃, b₃ ⟧
fe₁: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb₁
fe₂: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₂ p₃ fb₂
p₁ · (fb₁ · fb₂) ==> fe₁ · fe₂ · p₃
 exact (lassociator _ _ _
             • (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₁ ▹ _)
             • rassociator _ _ _
             • (_ ◃ mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₂)
             • lassociator _ _ _).
    
B: bicat
e₁, e₂, e₃, b₁, b₂, b₃: B
fb₁: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
fb₂: B ⟦ b₂, b₃ ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
p₃: B ⟦ e₃, b₃ ⟧
fe₁: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb₁
fe₂: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₂ p₃ fb₂
is_invertible_2cell
  ((((lassociator p₁ fb₁ fb₂
      • (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₁ ▹ fb₂))
     • rassociator fe₁ p₂ fb₂)
    • (fe₁ ◃ mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₂))
   • lassociator fe₁ fe₂ p₃)
 
B: bicat
e₁, e₂, e₃, b₁, b₂, b₃: B
fb₁: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
fb₂: B ⟦ b₂, b₃ ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
p₃: B ⟦ e₃, b₃ ⟧
fe₁: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb₁
fe₂: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₂ p₃ fb₂
is_invertible_2cell
  (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₁)
B: bicat
e₁, e₂, e₃, b₁, b₂, b₃: B
fb₁: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
fb₂: B ⟦ b₂, b₃ ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
p₃: B ⟦ e₃, b₃ ⟧
fe₁: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb₁
fe₂: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₂ p₃ fb₂
is_invertible_2cell
  (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₂)

      
B: bicat
e₁, e₂, e₃, b₁, b₂, b₃: B
fb₁: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
fb₂: B ⟦ b₂, b₃ ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
p₃: B ⟦ e₃, b₃ ⟧
fe₁: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb₁
fe₂: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₂ p₃ fb₂
is_invertible_2cell
  (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₁)
 apply property_from_invertible_2cell.
      
B: bicat
e₁, e₂, e₃, b₁, b₂, b₃: B
fb₁: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
fb₂: B ⟦ b₂, b₃ ⟧
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
p₃: B ⟦ e₃, b₃ ⟧
fe₁: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb₁
fe₂: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₂ p₃ fb₂
is_invertible_2cell
  (mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe₂)
 apply property_from_invertible_2cell.
Defined.

(**
 5. Cells of internal Street fibrations
 *)
Definition cell_of_internal_sfib_over_homot
           {B : bicat}
           {b₁ b₂ e₁ e₂ : B}
           {fb gb : b₁ --> b₂}
           (γ : fb ==> gb)
           {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
           {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
           {fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb}
           {ge : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb}
           (γe : fe ==> ge)
  : UU
  := mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe • (γe ▹ _)
     =
     (_ ◃ γ) • mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com ge.


Definition cell_of_internal_sfib_over
           {B : bicat}
           {b₁ b₂ e₁ e₂ : B}
           {fb gb : b₁ --> b₂}
           (γ : fb ==> gb)
           {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
           {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
           (fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb)
           (ge : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb)
  : UU
  := ∑ (γe : fe ==> ge), cell_of_internal_sfib_over_homot γ γe.

Definition make_cell_of_internal_sfib_over
           {B : bicat}
           {b₁ b₂ e₁ e₂ : B}
           {fb gb : b₁ --> b₂}
           {γ : fb ==> gb}
           {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
           {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
           {fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb}
           {ge : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb}
           (γe : fe ==> ge)
           (p : cell_of_internal_sfib_over_homot γ γe)
  : cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
  := (γe ,, p).

Coercion cell_of_cell_of_internal_sfib_over
         {B : bicat}
         {b₁ b₂ e₁ e₂ : B}
         {fb gb : b₁ --> b₂}
         {γ : fb ==> gb}
         {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
         {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
         {fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb}
         {ge : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb}
         (γe : cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge)
  : fe ==> ge
  := pr1 γe.

Definition cell_of_internal_sfib_over_eq
           {B : bicat}
           {b₁ b₂ e₁ e₂ : B}
           {fb gb : b₁ --> b₂}
           {γ : fb ==> gb}
           {p₁ : e₁ --> b₁}
           {p₂ : e₂ --> b₂}
           {fe : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb}
           {ge : mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb}
           (γe : cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge)
  : mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com fe • (γe ▹ _)
     =
     (_ ◃ γ) • mor_of_internal_sfib_over_com ge
  := pr2 γe.


B: bicat
b₁, b₂, e₁, e₂: B
fb, gb: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
γ: fb ==> gb
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
ge: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb
γe₁, γe₂: cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
p: pr1 γe₁ = γe₂
γe₁ = γe₂


B: bicat
b₁, b₂, e₁, e₂: B
fb, gb: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
γ: fb ==> gb
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
ge: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb
γe₁, γe₂: cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
p: pr1 γe₁ = γe₂
γe₁ = γe₂

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, e₁, e₂: B
fb, gb: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
γ: fb ==> gb
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
ge: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb
γe₁, γe₂: cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
p: pr1 γe₁ = γe₂
isPredicate (cell_of_internal_sfib_over_homot γ)
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, e₁, e₂: B
fb, gb: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
γ: fb ==> gb
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
ge: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb
γe₁, γe₂: cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
p: pr1 γe₁ = γe₂
pr1 γe₁ = pr1 γe₂

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, e₁, e₂: B
fb, gb: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
γ: fb ==> gb
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
ge: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb
γe₁, γe₂: cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
p: pr1 γe₁ = γe₂
isPredicate (cell_of_internal_sfib_over_homot γ)

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, e₁, e₂: B
fb, gb: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
γ: fb ==> gb
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
ge: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb
γe₁, γe₂: cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
p: pr1 γe₁ = γe₂
x: fe ==> ge
isaprop (cell_of_internal_sfib_over_homot γ x)

    apply cellset_property.
  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, e₁, e₂: B
fb, gb: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
γ: fb ==> gb
p₁: B ⟦ e₁, b₁ ⟧
p₂: B ⟦ e₂, b₂ ⟧
fe: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ fb
ge: mor_of_internal_sfib_over p₁ p₂ gb
γe₁, γe₂: cell_of_internal_sfib_over γ fe ge
p: pr1 γe₁ = γe₂
pr1 γe₁ = pr1 γe₂

  exact p.
Qed.
